Pradeshiya  sabha   NattaNdiya
It is hereby notified for the public information that it has been adopted under resolution No. 5-II moved at the General 
Conference held on 10.11.2022 at Pradeshiya Sabha Nattandiya that all the roads and thoroughfares for which legal action 
had not been filed in a proper Judicial Court before the date specified or roads and thoroughfares confirmed as the roads 
and thoroughfares that should be owned by Pradeshiya Sabha Nattandiya as per the Decree of a Judicial Court in which a 
case has been filed before the said date and not mentioned in the following Schedule from among the roads and 
thoroughfares given in the list of the Schedule of the notification published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2283/02 
and dated 06.06.2022 According to the resolution No. 05/V made at the Pradeshiya Sabha Conference held on 19.05.2022 
shall be confirmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Nattandiya in terms of orders made by the 
series of “ Orders on publications of notifications specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares 
maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 
and dated 30
th July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by Section 24(1) 
of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 0f 1987.
It is further notified that a list of said roads and thoroughfares has been included in the Schedule here to and 
all the roads and thoroughfares mentioned in that Schedule shall be considered as roads and thoroughfares owned by the 
Pradeshiya Sabha Nattandiya under Sub Section (5) of Section 24  of Pradeshiya Sabha Act.
 Roshan Nilantha Fernando, 
 (Attorney-at-Law)
 Chairman,
 Pradeshiya Sabha Nattandiya.
At Nattandiya Pradeshiya Sabha,
10th of November, 2022.

Resolution
Nattandiya Pradeshiya Sabha Proposes that the roads and thoroughfares for which legal actions had not been filed in a proper Judicial Court and 
not mentioned in the following Schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given in the list of the Schedule of the notification published in the 
Extraordinary Gazette No. 2283/02 and dated 06.06.2022, according to the resolution No. 05-V made at the Pradeshiya Sabha conference held on 19.05.2022, 
shall be confirmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Nattandiya in terms of orders made by the series of “Orders on publication of 
notifications specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” 
published by Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 and dated 30
th July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by 
Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 0f 1987.
